[10:04:01] <Toeol> (Xan) Armour Armour pieces that have been granted the boon of rarity will have additional damage mitigation. Each level of rarity grants another 3% damage mitigation on top of the static mitigation from the armour type. It has also been shown to increase the glance rate when compared to normal, non-rare, armour.
